ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;

        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {

  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

    //   init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) = init - absorbed
    // Since `ValidExecution(s, init)` guarantees non‑negativity at all prefixes,
    // in particular for the prefix of length `minK` we have
    //   init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0   =>   init >= absorbed

--- LLM RESPONSE (670 tokens, 6.17s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]) by auto;
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]) by auto;

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed) by auto;
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result by auto;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s| by auto;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0 by auto;
    assert init >= absorbed by auto;
  }
}

  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed

    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDe...

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile

  ghost var minK := 0;

    invariant 0 <= minK <= i

  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(t) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }

    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    // From the invariant at the end of the loop we have
    //   SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
    // and `absorbed` is the minimal initial pile size that keeps the pile non‑negative.
    // Any other valid initial pile size `init` must be at least `absorbed`.
    assert init >= absorbed;
    // Therefore the final pile size for `init` is
    //   init + SumDeltas(s) >= absorbed + SumDeltas(s)
    // which equals the result by the invariant `result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s)`.
    assert init + SumDeltas(s) >= absorbed + SumDeltas(s);
    assert FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result;
  }
}

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    // Using the invariant at the point where i == minK
    assert SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed;
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
    // Final pile size for this init
    assert FinalPileSize(s, init) == init + SumDeltas(s);
    // Compare with result
    assert init + SumDeltas(s) >= absorbed + SumDeltas(s);
    assert result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s);
    assert init + SumDeltas(s) >= result;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
</DAFNY

ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])

ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{

  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

{

ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile

  ghost var minK := 0;

    invariant absorbed >= 0

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0

    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed

}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {
    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}

ghost function Delta(c: char): int
{
  if c == '-' then -1 else 1
}

ghost function SumDeltas(s: seq<char>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else SumDeltas(s[..|s|-1]) + Delta(s[|s|-1])
}

// A valid execution: starting with `init` stones (>= 0), the pile
// never goes negative at any point during the sequence of operations.
ghost predicate ValidExecution(s: seq<char>, init: int)
{
  init >= 0 &&
  forall k | 0 <= k <= |s| :: init + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
}

ghost function FinalPileSize(s: seq<char>, init: int): int
{
  init + SumDeltas(s)
}

method PileOfStones(s: seq<char>) returns (result: int)
  // There exists a valid initial pile size that yields this result
  ensures exists init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) && FinalPileSize(s, init) == result
  // No valid initial pile size yields a smaller final pile
  ensures forall init: nat :: ValidExecution(s, init) ==> FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
{
  result := 0;
  var i := 0;
  ghost var absorbed := 0;
  ghost var minK := 0;

  while i < |s|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |s|
    invariant result >= 0
    invariant absorbed >= 0
    invariant result == absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..i])
    invariant forall k | 0 <= k <= i :: absorbed + SumDeltas(s[..k]) >= 0
    invariant 0 <= minK <= i
    invariant SumDeltas(s[..minK]) == -absorbed
  {

    // Inlined from SumDeltasAppend(s[..i], s[i])
    var t := (s[..i]) + [(s[i])];
    assert t[..|t|-1] == (s[..i]);
    assert SumDeltas(s[..i] + [s[i]]) == SumDeltas(s[..i]) + Delta(s[i]);

    if s[i] == '-' {
      if result > 0 {
        result := result - 1;
      } else {
        absorbed := absorbed + 1;
        minK := i + 1;
      }
    } else {
      result := result + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  // Witness for first postcondition
  assert ValidExecution(s, absorbed);
  assert FinalPileSize(s, absorbed) == result;

  // Second postcondition: minimality
  assert 0 <= minK <= |s|;
  forall init: nat | ValidExecution(s, init)
    ensures FinalPileSize(s, init) >= result
  {
    assert init + SumDeltas(s[..minK]) >= 0;
    assert init >= absorbed;
  }
}
